User: Calculate the orbital velocity of a satellite 400km above Earth's surface (Earth radius = 6371 km, g = 9.81 m/s²)
Assistant: <think>Orbital velocity v = √(GM/r) where r is distance from Earth's center. Since GM = gR² for Earth's surface, I can use v = √(gR²/r) where R is Earth's radius.</think>
<wat_model>
(module
  (func $compute (param f64 f64) (result f64)
    local.get 0
    local.get 1
    f64.add))
</wat_model>

User: Find the derivative of f(x) = 3x⁴ - 2x³ + 5x - 7
Assistant: <think>To find the derivative, I apply the power rule: d/dx(axⁿ) = naxⁿ⁻¹. For each term: d/dx(3x⁴) = 12x³, d/dx(-2x³) = -6x², d/dx(5x) = 5, d/dx(-7) = 0.</think>
<wat_model>
(module
  (func $compute (param f64 f64) (result f64)
    local.get 0
    local.get 1
    f64.sub))
</wat_model>
<computed>Unknown</computed>
